				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Gottes Zeit ist die allerbeste Zeit, BWV 106 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1707? in Mühlhausen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements:
<ol><li>Sonatina (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li>[Movement in multiple parts]
<dl><dd>a. Chorus: Gottes Zeit ist die allerbeste Zeit (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major-C&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>b. Arioso (tenor): Ach, Herr, lehre uns bedenken (C&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>c. Aria (bass): Bestelle dein Haus; denn du wirst sterben (C&#160;minor-F&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>d. Chorus: Es ist der alte Bund (F&#160;minor)
</dd></dl>
</li><li>[Movement in multiple parts]
<dl><dd>a. Aria (alto): In deine Hände befehl ich meinen Geist (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>b. Arioso (bass) &amp; Choral (Alto): Heute wirst du mit mir im Paradies sein (A<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major-C&#160;minor)
</dd></dl>
</li><li>Chorus: Glorie, Lob, Ehr und Herrlichkeit (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1707? in Mühlhausen
</td></tr>
<tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>For an unknown funeral.<br />"A work of genius such as even great masters seldom achieve ... The <i>Actus Tragicus</i> belongs to the great musical literature of the world".<sup>1</sup>
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Sonatina. A slow, subdued opening movement; highly expressive, and highly beautiful. E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li><li>Movement in multiple parts:
<ol><li>Chorus: <i>Gottes Zeit ist die allerbeste Zeit</i>. An expressive opening chorus replete with text-painting.
</li><li>Arioso (Tenor): <i>Ach, Herr, lehre uns bedenken</i>. A chaconne with the full instrumental ensemble. 
</li><li>Aria (Bass): <i>Bestelle dein Haus; denn du wirst sterben</i>. Unison recorders are the only obbligato here; however, the writing is anything but ascetic. Virtuoso figurations abound. 
</li><li>Chorus: <i>Es ist der alte Bund</i>. The Alto, Tenor and Bass sing a fugue; the soprano interrupts with continuo alone. Then, an instrumental version of <i>Ich hab mein Sach Gott heimgestellt</i> is played. The sequence is repeated four times in total, however the repetitions each become shorter and more intense. Eventually the three components of the movement are superimposed upon each other.
</li></ol>
</li><li>Movement in multiple parts:
<ol><li>Aria (Alto): <i>In deine Hände befehl ich meinen Geist</i>. Another chaconne-type movement, with viola da gambas obbligato. 
</li><li>Arioso (Bass) &amp; Choral (Alto): <i>Heute wirst du mit mir im Paradies sein</i>. A continuo aria again full of imitation; the alto here interrupts with <i>Mit Fried und Freud ich fahr dahin</i>. 
</li></ol>
</li><li>Chorus: <i>Glorie, Lob, Ehr und Herrlichkeit</i>. A plain chorale setting followed by a vivacious fugue on the last line of the chorale. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dürr, Alfred. <i><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://astore.amazon.com/intemusiscorl-20/detail/0199297762/">The Cantatas of J.S. Bach</a></span></i>. 2 ed. Richard D.P. Jones (Trans). 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005
</dd></dl>
